---
title: Release Notes
---

# Release Notes

## 1.0.0-rc.120

**Changes**

- Command + down opens the current selection in the archive or inbox (#97)
- Update the wizard toolbar icon and add tooltips (#99)
- Launch the Rules Wizard and Quick Look from the context menu (#104)
- Add 'Edit' to the context menu in the Rules settings tab (#114)macOS
- Add a button to add text to rules (#123)macOS
- Enable directory creation from the directory picker (#127)macOS
- Multiple inbox locations (#129)macOS
- Sort by the file creation date if no date can be found in the filename (#166)
- Automatically offer dates from within the PDF in the date picker of the Rules Wizard (#167)
- Copy file names from the context menu (#202)
- Reorder rule variables (#220)
- Hit enter to select the matching rule in the Rules Wizard (#222)
- Filter rules by the archive name as well as the rule name (#223)
- Target macOS Ventura (#229)
- Add an about screen with acknowledgements to the Mac app (#257)
- Increase the version number to 1.0 (#261)
- Add an about screen to the iOS app (#309)
- Recognise .fileaway rules files (#356)
- Show and manage inboxes and archives in iOS (#364)
- Show a sheet when tapping on files on iOS (#376)
- Add a simple rule editor to the iOS app (#382)
- Pick which file types to display on macOS (#440)
- Select file types on iOS (#449)
- Quick access list of recently used rules (#467)
- Open files from the application menu (#483)
- Show a document preview in the rule wizard on iOS (#484)
- Select folders from the main menu and command palette (#495)
- Perform actions on selected files on iOS (#499)

**Fixes**

- Make double-clicking to open rules in settings more reliable (#94)
- Fixed a crash when closing the Rules Wizard (#101)
- Move Wizard toolbar button should be disabled when no items are selected (#102)
- Update the Rules Wizard title to ‘Select Rule’ (#105)macOS
- Put the Rules Wizard first in the toolbar (#107)macOS
- Duplicate and delete context menu items act on all selected rules in the Rules editor (#140)macOS
- Set the initial directory when picking rules destinations (#143)macOS
- Add directory icons to the archives in the Rules settings tab (#146)macOS
- Only strip dates at the beginning of filenames (#161)
- Correct display name for iCloud Drive and other special directories (#164)
- Equal width for the location add/remove buttons (#165)
- Correctly extract both dates from date ranges (#168)
- Target macOS 12 Monterey (#214)
- Focus the search field when launching the rules wizard (#215)
- Improve layout of the +/- buttons in the Settings rules list (#216)
- Better layout of the list buttons in the rule editor (#219)
- Disable the rule list edit buttons when no items are selected (#221)
- Incorrect display of the add/remove rule buttons (#230)
- Make the variable add/remove buttons clickable (#249)
- Improve the initial layout of the rule editor (#250)
- Improve context menu handling in the rule editor (#251)
- Update the macOS icon (#256)
- Add a privacy policy (#262)
- Add licenses to the about screen (#263)
- Update to the new SwiftUI list multi-selection support (#264)
- Use the new SwiftUI mechanism for opening new windows (#265)
- Update the rules toolbar icon and add a label (#273)
- Apply rules to multiple files at once (#275)
- Add a label to the delete toolbar item (#277)
- Make the full path less prominent (#278)
- Clean up the selection when files are removed from the directory (#279)
- Don't show duplicates in the suggested dates list (#282)
- Improve file selection reliability (#283)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard (#284)
- Use the new grouped form style in the wizard and offer file creation date (#285)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard rule list (#286)
- Improved keyboard navigation support for rule picker (#287)
- Show the commit id in the about screen (#292)
- Remove duplicate Diligence license from the about window (#293)
- Consistent placeholder formatting in the file list (#300)
- Show a disabled toolbar when no directory is selected (#301)
- Correct the color of the placeholder background (#303)
- Ensure the Diligence license can be shown from the about screen (#304)
- Use common build numbers for macOS and iOS (#307)
- Build and publish the iOS app (#308)
- Add an icon to the about screen (#310)
- Remove the legacy destination from the main view (#311)
- Change the settings button to a gear (#315)
- Re-enable the macOS sidebar context menu (#326)
- Don't share state between different windows (#345)
- Rename the rules files to 'Rules.fileaway' to make them more obvious (#351)
- Store the UUID and name directly alongside each rule (#357)
- Update the iOS configuration format to match macOS (#358)
- Ensure the iOS app stores rules in the correct format (#359)
- Introduce a cross-platform file picker (#362)
- Show settings on iOS (#366)
- Restore the accent color to the iOS app (#368)
- Support deleting locations on iOS (#370)
- Add Fileaway license to the about view (#371)
- Adding a second location fails (#372)
- Show an icon alongside the delete location context menu item (#373)
- Prefer plain list style in the directory view on iOS (#374)
- Use large titles in the directory view on iOS (#375)
- Navigate between files while previewing with Quick Look (#378)
- Small aesthetic improvements to the iOS rules editor (#383)
- Save the locations on iOS (#387)
- Add a link to the Fileaway website (#388)
- Show relative paths of files to reduce clutter (#389)
- Rename the remove location action from 'Delete' to 'Remove' (#392)
- Open the first inbox by default (#401)
- Simplify the appearance of the wizard rule view (#402)
- Only update the focused rule when the filter is non-empty (#403)
- Clean up the appearance of the macOS rules wizard (#404)
- Date variables don't expand correctly (#406)
- Add a rule picker to the iOS wizard (#412)
- Show the rule form on iOS (#413)
- Show file previews on iOS (#414)
- File preview doesn't work on the iOS rule form (#419)
- Support deleting files on iOS (#421)
- Colorize the variables in the iOS rules editor to help differentiate them (#425)
- Improve the appearance of the variable selector on iOS (#426)
- Bring the macOS rule editor in-line with the iOS experience (#431)
- Edit rules from the iOS settings view (#432)
- Show file counts on inbox rows (#433)
- Restore icons with improved performance (#436)
- Show a progress spinner during initial directory load (#437)
- 100% CPU usage when idle (#438)
- Show icons for folders in settings on macOS (#441)
- Show the destination folder name in the rules list on iOS (#442)
- Support pull-to-refresh in folders on iOS (#443)
- Folders shouldn't be scrollable on iOS when loading (#445)
- Update the default rule destination to 'Paperwork' (#450)
- Dismiss the iOS wizard on completion (#451)
- Set the application badge count on iOS (#452)
- Don't log unnecessarily when requesting notification permission (#464)
- Show relative destination in the rule form (#465)
- Update the directory views when moving files on iOS (#466)
- Use the token appearance for variables in the rules editor (#468)
- Wrap variable tokens in the rules editor (#469)
- Ensure dates in file rows don't wrap on smaller screens (#470)
- Use short dates in keeping with Mail.app (#471)
- Update the iOS add folder button text to 'Add Folder...' (#473)
- Store recently used rule on form submit (#474)
- Separate fields for setting the rule destination folder and filename (#476)
- Cap the number of recent rules at 3 (#479)
- Show a title when the header has scrolled out of view in the iOS about view (#480)
- Icons are blurry on iOS (#481)
- Refresh iOS folders when foregrounding the app (#482)
- Don't show a context menu in the iOS folder sidebar (#493)
- Disable selection in compact size classes on iOS and iPadOS (#494)
- Crash showing settings on macOS (#496)
- Support interactive edit mode on iOS in the directory view (#498)
- Duplicating rules incorrectly duplicates identifiers (#501)
- Rules variable are incorrectly updated after cancelling edit on iOS (#509)
- Short date variables incorrectly include the day (#511)
- Move and reveal files from the main menu and command palette (#512)
- Store the selected folder (#513)
- Simplify the rule editor on macOS and iOS (#514)
- Increase variable color palette and show variable colors in move form (#516)
- Directory views don't notice changes when moving or deleting folders (#517)
- Support manually reordering locations (#520)
- Unable to add archive folders on iOS (#525)
- Update the copyright notice for 2023 (#529)
- Update the Diligence and Interact licenses (#530)
- Thank Lukas 🙏🏻 (#531)
- Support drag-and-drop in the file list (#533)
- Update the icon (#534)
- Update TestFlight build (#536)
- Update provisioning profiles and certificates (#537)
- Update the App Store Connect API keys (#539)
- Update TestFlight builds (#541)
- Update copyright to Jason Morley (#544)
- Show a friendlier placeholder for empty folders (#551)

- Ensure the iOS app stores rules in the correct format (#359)

- Simplify the appearance of the wizard rule view (#402)
- Only update the focused rule when the filter is non-empty (#403)
- Clean up the appearance of the macOS rules wizard (#404)
- Date variables don't expand correctly (#406)
- Add a rule picker to the iOS wizard (#412)
- Show the rule form on iOS (#413)
- Show file previews on iOS (#414)
- File preview doesn't work on the iOS rule form (#419)
- Support deleting files on iOS (#421)
- Colorize the variables in the iOS rules editor to help differentiate them (#425)
- Improve the appearance of the variable selector on iOS (#426)
- Bring the macOS rule editor in-line with the iOS experience (#431)
- Edit rules from the iOS settings view (#432)
- Show file counts on inbox rows (#433)
- Restore icons with improved performance (#436)
- Show a progress spinner during initial directory load (#437)
- 100% CPU usage when idle (#438)
- Show icons for folders in settings on macOS (#441)
- Show the destination folder name in the rules list on iOS (#442)
- Support pull-to-refresh in folders on iOS (#443)
- Folders shouldn't be scrollable on iOS when loading (#445)

- Correctly extract both dates from date ranges (#168)

- Make the variable add/remove buttons clickable (#249)

- Improve context menu handling in the rule editor (#251)

- Add a privacy policy (#262)
- Add licenses to the about screen (#263)
- Update to the new SwiftUI list multi-selection support (#264)
- Use the new SwiftUI mechanism for opening new windows (#265)
- Update the rules toolbar icon and add a label (#273)
- Apply rules to multiple files at once (#275)
- Add a label to the delete toolbar item (#277)
- Make the full path less prominent (#278)
- Clean up the selection when files are removed from the directory (#279)
- Don't show duplicates in the suggested dates list (#282)
- Improve file selection reliability (#283)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard (#284)
- Use the new grouped form style in the wizard and offer file creation date (#285)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard rule list (#286)
- Improved keyboard navigation support for rule picker (#287)
- Show the commit id in the about screen (#292)
- Remove duplicate Diligence license from the about window (#293)
- Consistent placeholder formatting in the file list (#300)
- Show a disabled toolbar when no directory is selected (#301)
- Correct the color of the placeholder background (#303)

- Build and publish the iOS app (#308)
- Add an icon to the about screen (#310)
- Remove the legacy destination from the main view (#311)
- Change the settings button to a gear (#315)
- Re-enable the macOS sidebar context menu (#326)
- Don't share state between different windows (#345)
- Rename the rules files to 'Rules.fileaway' to make them more obvious (#351)
- Store the UUID and name directly alongside each rule (#357)
- Update the iOS configuration format to match macOS (#358)
- Ensure the iOS app stores rules in the correct format (#359)
- Introduce a cross-platform file picker (#362)
- Show settings on iOS (#366)
- Restore the accent color to the iOS app (#368)
- Support deleting locations on iOS (#370)

- Adding a second location fails (#372)
- Show an icon alongside the delete location context menu item (#373)
- Prefer plain list style in the directory view on iOS (#374)
- Use large titles in the directory view on iOS (#375)

- Small aesthetic improvements to the iOS rules editor (#383)
- Save the locations on iOS (#387)
- Add a link to the Fileaway website (#388)
- Show relative paths of files to reduce clutter (#389)
- Rename the remove location action from 'Delete' to 'Remove' (#392)
- Open the first inbox by default (#401)
- Simplify the appearance of the wizard rule view (#402)
- Only update the focused rule when the filter is non-empty (#403)

- Correctly extract both dates from date ranges (#168)
- Target macOS 12 Monterey (#214)
- Focus the search field when launching the rules wizard (#215)
- Improve layout of the +/- buttons in the Settings rules list (#216)
- Better layout of the list buttons in the rule editor (#219)
- Disable the rule list edit buttons when no items are selected (#221)
- Incorrect display of the add/remove rule buttons (#230)
- Make the variable add/remove buttons clickable (#249)
- Improve the initial layout of the rule editor (#250)
- Improve context menu handling in the rule editor (#251)
- Update the macOS icon (#256)
- Add a privacy policy (#262)
- Add licenses to the about screen (#263)
- Update to the new SwiftUI list multi-selection support (#264)
- Use the new SwiftUI mechanism for opening new windows (#265)
- Update the rules toolbar icon and add a label (#273)
- Apply rules to multiple files at once (#275)
- Add a label to the delete toolbar item (#277)
- Make the full path less prominent (#278)
- Clean up the selection when files are removed from the directory (#279)
- Don't show duplicates in the suggested dates list (#282)
- Improve file selection reliability (#283)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard (#284)
- Use the new grouped form style in the wizard and offer file creation date (#285)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard rule list (#286)
- Improved keyboard navigation support for rule picker (#287)
- Show the commit id in the about screen (#292)
- Remove duplicate Diligence license from the about window (#293)
- Consistent placeholder formatting in the file list (#300)
- Show a disabled toolbar when no directory is selected (#301)
- Correct the color of the placeholder background (#303)
- Ensure the Diligence license can be shown from the about screen (#304)
- Use common build numbers for macOS and iOS (#307)
- Build and publish the iOS app (#308)
- Add an icon to the about screen (#310)
- Remove the legacy destination from the main view (#311)
- Change the settings button to a gear (#315)
- Re-enable the macOS sidebar context menu (#326)
- Don't share state between different windows (#345)
- Rename the rules files to 'Rules.fileaway' to make them more obvious (#351)
- Store the UUID and name directly alongside each rule (#357)
- Update the iOS configuration format to match macOS (#358)
- Ensure the iOS app stores rules in the correct format (#359)
- Introduce a cross-platform file picker (#362)
- Show settings on iOS (#366)
- Restore the accent color to the iOS app (#368)
- Support deleting locations on iOS (#370)
- Add Fileaway license to the about view (#371)
- Adding a second location fails (#372)
- Show an icon alongside the delete location context menu item (#373)
- Prefer plain list style in the directory view on iOS (#374)

- Sort by the file creation date if no date can be found in the filename (#166)

- Add an about screen to the iOS app (#309)
- Recognise .fileaway rules files (#356)
- Show and manage inboxes and archives in iOS (#364)

- Introduce a cross-platform file picker (#362)

- Only strip dates at the beginning of filenames (#161)

- Correctly extract both dates from date ranges (#168)

- Add licenses to the about screen (#263)

- Update the rules toolbar icon and add a label (#273)
- Apply rules to multiple files at once (#275)
- Add a label to the delete toolbar item (#277)
- Make the full path less prominent (#278)
- Clean up the selection when files are removed from the directory (#279)
- Don't show duplicates in the suggested dates list (#282)
- Improve file selection reliability (#283)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard (#284)
- Use the new grouped form style in the wizard and offer file creation date (#285)
- Clean up the appearance of the rules wizard rule list (#286)
- Improved keyboard navigation support for rule picker (#287)

- Use common build numbers for macOS and iOS (#307)
- Build and publish the iOS app (#308)

- Remove the legacy destination from the main view (#311)
- Change the settings button to a gear (#315)
- Re-enable the macOS sidebar context menu (#326)
- Don't share state between different windows (#345)
